   <!-- Start Content Area --> 
   <div id="main"> 
    <h3 style="text-align: center"><span style="font-family: Tahoma"><span style="font-size: large">Welcome to Student Business Services and Main Cashiers&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></h3> 
    <p>&nbsp;</p> 
    <p style="text-align: center"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000"><span style="font-size: medium">1098-T Tuition&nbsp;Statements for 2013 are now available online at <a href="http://www.1098T.com">www.1098T.com</a>&nbsp;to print.&nbsp; Please call 877-467-3821 for questions.</span></span></strong></p> 
    <p>&nbsp;</p> 
    <p><span style="font-size: medium">Our highly trained staff strives to provide excellent customer service in the areas of cashiering operations, billing receivables, disbursement of student aid, maintenance and collection of student loans and campus receivables.&nbsp; Please take advantage of this web environment providing information encompassing all of our services.&nbsp; Student Business Services and Main Cashiers will strive to meet your continuing needs and look forward to being of service to everyone in the campus community.</span></p> 
    <p>&nbsp;</p> 
    <p style="text-align: left; margin-left: 40px">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<img alt="" width="500" height="250" src="/UCR1.jpg" /></p> 
    <p style="text-align: center">&nbsp;</p> 
    <table cellpadding="5" width="100%" border="0"> 
     <tbody> 
      <tr> 
       <td valign="top" width="50%" colspan="2" style="text-align: center"> <p style="text-align: left"><span style="font-size: medium">Student Business Services&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong>Main Cashiers Office<br /> Student Services Bldg, HOSS&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Student Services Bldg, Rm 1111<br /> Monday - Friday: 9 am&nbsp;- 5 pm&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Monday - Friday: 9 am&nbsp;- 12 pm &amp; 1 pm&nbsp;- 3 pm<br /> Phone: (951) 827-3204&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Phone: (951) 827-3208<br /> Fax: (951) 827-3576&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Fax: (951) 827-7976</span></p> <p style="text-align: left; margin-left: 160px"><span style="font-size: medium">Email: </span><a href="mailto:sbsofc@ucr.edu"><span style="font-size: medium">sbsofc@ucr.edu</span></a><span style="font-size: medium">&nbsp;</span></p> </td> 
      </tr> 
      <tr> 
       <td colspan="2" align="center"> <p style="text-align: left; margin-left: 160px"><span style="font-size: medium"><u>Main Cashiers Mailing Address</u>:</span></p> <p style="text-align: left; margin-left: 160px"><span style="font-size: medium">UCR Main Cashiers Office<br /> 900 University Avenue<br /> Student Services Bldg, Rm 1111<br /> Riverside, CA&nbsp; 92521</span></p> </td> 
      </tr> 
     </tbody> 
    </table> 
    <p style="text-align: left">&nbsp;</p> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 80px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">The Main Cashiers Office walk-up window service is available:</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 200px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">Monday through Friday</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 200px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">9 am - 12 pm AND 1 pm&nbsp;- 3 pm</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 200px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">Closed from Noon - 1 pm</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 40px">
     &nbsp;
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 120px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">All <em>in-person</em> payments are due by 3 pm PST.</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 40px">
     &nbsp;
    </div> 
    <div style="margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: left; margin-top: 0in; margin-right: 0in">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">Payments may be made via&nbsp;GROWL or check/money order left in the Cashiers drop box <em><u>until 4 pm</u></em>.</span>&nbsp; 
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">(Drop box is located on the outside of the Student Services Building.)&nbsp;</span>
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 40px">
     &nbsp;
    </div> 
    <div style="text-align: left; margin: 0in 0in 0pt 80px">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt">Departments please plan the timing of your deposits accordingly.</span>
    </div> 
    <p>&nbsp;</p> 
   </div>

         <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
          <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
           <div class="hd">
            <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
             <div class="headline">
              <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/why-boys-boys-no-longer-excuse-195700043.html" mapleultparams="pkg=a1ab8874-5f42-3e40-8d01-f900a23a4faa;ver=0cec3a02-bf12-11e1-ac4e-9a617efc5af5;pos=1">Why &quot;Boys Will Be Boys&quot; Can No Longer Be an Excuse</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/diane-mizota-host-of-this-week-in-m-o-m--ycn-1137181/" mapleultparams="pos=1">Diane Mizota, Host Of This Week In M.o.m.</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/moments-of-motherhood/">Moments Of Motherhood</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2012-06-25T19:57:00Z">Mon, Jun 25, 2012 3:57 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/moments-of-motherhood/why-boys-boys-no-longer-excuse-195700043.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
           </div>
           <div class="bd">
            <p></p> 
            <p> </p>
            <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-right" style="width:310px;">
             <img src="http://l.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/afVbY2sBMvRwQ0J5bLt8Nw--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2410528.0" id="2410528" name="2410528" alt="" height="207" width="310" />
            </div>
            <p></p> 
            <p> Watching the viral video of four boys bullying a 68 year-old woman on the school bus is every parent's nightmare- especially mothers of boys. In an interview with Anderson Cooper, Karen Klein, the bullied bus monitor, shared: </p> 
            <p> &quot;I'm sure they don't act that way at home, but you never know what they're going to do when they're out of the house.&quot; </p> 
            <p> I watched in horror of how they treated this woman, and my head was swimming- with fear that <em>Lord of the Flies</em> is being reenacted on school buses and playgrounds daily. With hatred for the messages engrained in our culture that measure a person's worth by the size of their waistline or their wallet. With disgust for the graphic, sexually violent language used so flippantly to debase a woman with hate. With sadness for the boys' lack of conscience that what they are doing is hurtful and wrong. With contempt for the rigid code of manhood that constrains how they are programmed to connect with one another and themselves. </p> 
            <p> But mostly I j</p>...

             </div>
            </div>
            <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/charlene-prince-birkeland-shine-staff-ycn-1139393/" mapleultparams="pos=2">Charlene Prince Birkeland, Shine Staff</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/moments-of-motherhood/">Moments Of Motherhood</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2012-06-22T21:13:00Z">Fri, Jun 22, 2012 5:13 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/moments-of-motherhood/quiet-time-5-free-healthy-whole-family-activities-211300382.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>

           <div class="bd">
            <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-left" style="width:310px;">
             <img src="http://l1.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/cpHA0OR98TdRwzFLbEbzjQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2408332.0" title="Sunday Morning: Go for a hike!" id="2408332" alt="Sunday Morning: Go for a hike!" name="2408332" height="207" width="310" />
             <p class="legend">Sunday Morning: Go for a hike!</p>
            </div>Weekends 
            <em>should</em> be blissful, free of the crazy chaos that usually takes place Monday through Friday. But Saturdays can still be filled with shuttling the kids back and forth between practices, parties and play dates -- that antithesis of bliss. If you find yourself eager to etch out quiet, peaceful time with your family, you need a plan. 
            <br />
            <p></p> 
            <p> Here's one: Set aside your Sunday morning for special family time, and try one of these five mellow activities:</p> 
            <p> -<strong>Camp out!</strong> Or at least pretend you did! When you wake up, fire up the grill and pretend your camping. Serve up a delicious and healthy breakfast (<a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.crazedparent.org/2009/07/dispatch-from-the-test-kitchen-camping-edition-a-birds-nest.html">bird's nest anyone</a>?) in the backyard. </p> 
            <p> -<strong>Have a breakfast picnic in the park</strong>. Grab a blanket, pack a simple breakfast, some books and games, and walk to a nearby park for morning eats and fun with the kids.</p> 
            <p> -<strong>Walk, bike, or scoot to your local's farmer's market</strong>. Sample sweet fruits and veggies bursting with flavor. </p> 
            <p> -<strong style="font-size:14px;">Go for a hike</strong>. Tour beautiful trails in your area and enjoy the sights,</p>...
            <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/quiet-time-5-free-healthy-whole-family-activities-211300382.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=8bdd2e32-c410-3f79-9325-1df6c8e67c18;ver=37baf0d7-bcbb-11e1-9ffb-a03b764a27ff;pos=2">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
           </div>

           <div class="hd">
            <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
             <div class="headline">
              <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/birthday-party-overload-8230-175000509.html" mapleultparams="pkg=19abaf51-480d-3683-832c-8ca0f676246f;ver=8bb936c2-ba40-11e1-ad3f-d14f2d655436;pos=4">Birthday Party Overload…</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/diane-mizota-host-of-this-week-in-m-o-m--ycn-1137181/" mapleultparams="pos=4">Diane Mizota, Host Of This Week In M.o.m.</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/moments-of-motherhood/">Moments Of Motherhood</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2012-06-19T17:50:00Z">Tue, Jun 19, 2012 1:50 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/moments-of-motherhood/birthday-party-overload-8230-175000509.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
           </div>
           <div class="bd">
            <p></p> 
            <p> </p>
            <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-middle" style="width:310px;">
             <img src="http://l2.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/A5cUpKED77BqxdW4nNrgBg--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2404394.0" title="Birthday Party Overload..." id="2404394" name="2404394" alt="Birthday Party Overload..." height="207" width="310" />
             <p class="legend">Birthday Party Overload...</p>
            </div>
            <p></p> 
            <p> Kids' birthday parties are getting out of hand! In today's celebrity-obsessed, competitive hyper-parenting atmosphere, we are spending thousands and even tens of thousands of dollars on kids' parties. What happened to cake, ice cream and pin the tail on the donkey? </p> 
            <p> I just finished throwing my son a party for his 5 th birthday, and I'm wiped. I tried to keep it simple by having it at home, yet I still feel as if I threw a small wedding reception, and I've got the receipts to prove it. My first mistake? Inviting about 15 kids, which sounds manageable, until you remember that each of those kids brings one or two parents each and maybe a sibling. Add in family and neighbors, and 15 kids quickly multiplies into a party of 50. Now, you've got to feed, hydrate and entertain 50 people. Yikes! </p> 
            <p> Our party was not over the top. We had a bouncy house, pizza, fruit…and Jedi Training. But when you factor in party favors, rental chairs and tables, cake, plates, it all adds up. For this 2 h</p>...
            <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/birthday-party-overload-8230-175000509.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=19abaf51-480d-3683-832c-8ca0f676246f;ver=8bb936c2-ba40-11e1-ad3f-d14f2d655436;pos=4">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <hr /></li>
         <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
          <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
           <div class="hd">
            <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
             <div class="headline">
              <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/whats-summer-bag-6-things-mom-always-hand-144800648.html" mapleultparams="pkg=2369d6c2-39a1-3c02-8f0a-22fa76d63bde;ver=8c2dcbbd-b996-11e1-bfb7-bfd1b118c466;pos=5">What's in Your Summer Bag? 6 Things a Mom Should Always Have on Hand</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/charlene-prince-birkeland-shine-staff-ycn-1139393/" mapleultparams="pos=5">Charlene Prince Birkeland, Shine Staff</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/moments-of-motherhood/">Moments Of Motherhood</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2012-06-17T14:48:00Z">Sun, Jun 17, 2012 10:48 AM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/moments-of-motherhood/whats-summer-bag-6-things-mom-always-hand-144800648.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
           </div>
           <div class="bd">
            <p><br /></p>
            <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-left" style="width:310px;">
             <img src="http://l2.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/xvYBs0jbNjUqIigyYMs2qQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2401434.0" title="What do you carry in your summer bag?" id="2401434" alt="What do you carry in your summer bag?" name="2401434" height="247" width="310" />
             <p class="legend">What do you carry in your summer bag?</p>
            </div>A 
            <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/femail/article-501871/The-average-womans-handbag-weighs-FIVE-bags-sugar.html">2007 study reported</a> that the average woman's handbag weighed nearly seven pounds. Apparently, the stat went 
            <a href="http://www.pcmag.com/article2/0,2817,2358090,00.asp">down in 2010 to three pounds</a>, as we started carrying smaller tech gadgets. But those numbers can't be accurate for moms, especially over the summer. 
            <br />
            <br /> Does the content of your handbag change in the summer? Mine does. 
            <a rel="nofollow" href="http://epiphaniebags.com/index.html#/shoplyric/"><span>It</span></a> became noticeably heavier this past week. Like 
            <a rel="nofollow" href="http://petitelefant.com/whats-in-your-purse-series-week-87-too-much/">Allison over at Petit Elefant</a>, I suddenly was carrying more 
            <em>stuff</em>. 
            <em>Summer stuff</em>...for my kids. 
            <br />
            <br /> Along with my own personal items -- sunglasses, makeup, wallet, iWhatever, a notebook and pens -- I have several things I only keep in my purse during the summer months. And I'm guessing you'll likely have these items in your bag as well. Check out these summer &quot;mom bag&quot; essentials: 
            <br />
            <br />
            <strong>Snacks.</strong> Kids seem to be hungry 
            <em>all the time</em> during the summer. Be sure to carry simple snacks at all times. I usually tote apple slices, cheese sticks and a few 
            <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.clifbar.com/food/products_clif_kid_zbar/">Z Bars</a>. If my kids don't eat them, I will! 
            <br />
            <strong><br /> A water bottle</strong>. Kids play hard and you 
            <p></p>...
            <a href="/moments-of-motherhood/whats-summer-bag-6-things-mom-always-hand-144800648.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=2369d6c2-39a1-3c02-8f0a-22fa76d63bde;ver=8c2dcbbd-b996-11e1-bfb7-bfd1b118c466;pos=5">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <hr /></li>
        </ul>
       </div>

              <td valign="top"><p class="COLUMNheadline">The CALDER QUARTET<br /> <br /> <br /> </p> <p class="COLUMNcontent2">Like the iconic mobiles, the superb quartet relies on the motion of interrelated shapes to balance one piece of music against another so that each reveals something new.</p> <p class="COLUMNcontent2">&nbsp;</p> <p class="COLUMNcontent2"><span class="LINEUPdate">FREE on Feb. 17, 2013, 4 pm <br /> </span> </p> <p class="LINEUPdate"><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/post/33237662149/the-calder-quartet" class="LINEUPdate2">Learn More</a><br /> <br /> </p></td> 
              <td valign="top" class="COLUMNheadline"><p class="COLUMNheadline">David Wax Museum<br /> </p> <p class="COLUMNcontent2">&nbsp;</p> <p class="COLUMNcontent2">Playing an exuberant blend of traditional Mexican folk with American roots and indie rock, band members <strong>David Wax</strong> and <strong>Suz Slezak</strong> channel their border crossing sensibilities to create a &quot;Mexo-Americana&quot; aesthetic.<br /> <span class="LINEUPdate"><br /> FREE on March 7, 2013, 8 pm</span><br /> </p> <p class="LINEUPdate2"><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/post/42030605188/david-wax-museum-march-7- 8pm" class="LINEUPdate">Learn More</a><br /></p></td> 
              <td valign="top"><p class="COLUMNheadline">JOSH KORNBLUTH, The Mathematics of Change </p> <p class="COLUMNcontent"><span class="COLUMNcontent2"><br /> A comic monologue that recounts the uproarious experiences of a Princeton University would-be math whiz who discovers his limits in freshman calculus. </span></p> <p class="COLUMNcontent"><br /> </p> <p class="COLUMNcontent"><span class="LINEUPdate">FREE on April 21, 2013, 4 pm <br /> </span></p> <p class="LINEUPdate"><span class="LINEUPdate2"><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/post/33237316323/josh-kornbluth-comic-monologuist-and-filmmaker">Learn More</a></span><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/&nbsp;"><br /> </a><br /> </p></td>
